Resonance</b> for all other Characters.

<div class="perkDescHeader divTableHeader">Description</div>
<div class="perkDesc divTableCell">Overwhelming pain reverberates outwards.
<p>At the start of the Trial, <b><span class="luaClr clr clr2" style="color: #e8c252;">4 random Hooks</span></b> are changed into <b>Scourge Hooks</b>:
</p><ul><li>The <a href="/wiki/Aura" class="mw-redirect" title="Aura">Auras</a><span class="iconLink" style="vertical-align: middle; padding: 0 0 0 0"><span style="width:32px;max-height: 32px" class="pcView pcIconLink"><span class="tooltip linkIncluded borderless"><span class="tooltipBaseText iconless"><a href="/wiki/Aura" title="Aura"><img alt="IconHelp auras" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="64" height="64" data-image-name="IconHelp auras.png" data-image-key="IconHelp_auras.png" data-relevant="0" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/deadbydaylight_gamepedia_en/images/0/03/IconHelp_auras.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/64?cb=20170907143115" class="lazyload" /></a></span><span class="tooltiptext flex flexCenter"><span class="tooltipTextWrapper"><a href="/wiki/Aura" title="Aura"><img alt="IconHelp auras" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="96" height="96" data-image-name="IconHelp auras.png" data-image-key="IconHelp_auras.png" data-relevant="0" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/deadbydaylight_gamepedia_en/images/0/03/IconHelp_auras.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/96?cb=20170907143115" class="lazyload" /></a></span></span></span></span><span class="mobileView mobileIconLink"><a href="/wiki/Aura" title="Aura"><img alt="IconHelp auras" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="32" height="32" data-image-name="IconHelp auras.png" data-image-key="IconHelp_auras.png" data-relevant="0" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/deadbydaylight_gamepedia_en/images/0/03/IconHelp_auras.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/32?cb=20170907143115" class="lazyload" /></a></span></span> of <b>Scourge Hooks</b> are revealed to you in <b><span class="luaClr clr clr16" style="color: #ffffff;">white</span></b>.</li></ul>
<p>You start the Trial with <b><span class="luaClr clr clr6" style="color: #ff8800;">4 Tokens</span></b> on <i>Scourge Hook: Pain Resonance</i>.
</p><p>Each time a Survivor is hooked on a <b>Scourge Hook</b> for the first time, <b><span class="luaClr clr clr8" style="color: #d41c1c;">1 Token</span></b> is consumed and the following effects apply:
</p><ul><li>The <a href="/wiki/Generator" class="mw-redirect" title="Generator">Generator</a><span class="iconLink" style="vertical-align: middle; padding: 0 0 0 0"><span style="width:32px;max-height: 32px" class="pcView pcIconLink"><span class="tooltip linkIncluded borderless"><span class="tooltipBaseText iconless"><a href="/wiki/Generator" title="Generator"><img alt="IconHelpLoading generators" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="64" height="64" data-image-name="IconHelpLoading generators.png" data-image-key="IconHelpLoading_generators.png" data-relevant="0" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/deadbydaylight_gamepedia_en/images/c/c4/IconHelpLoading_generators.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/64?cb=20170625095337" class="lazyload" /></a></span><span class="tooltiptext flex flexCenter"><span class="tooltipTextWrapper"><a href="/wiki/Generator" title="Generator"><img alt="IconHelpLoading generators" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="96" height="96" data-image-name="IconHelpLoading generators.png" data-image-key="IconHelpLoading_generators.png" data-relevant="0" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/deadbydaylight_gamepedia_en/images/c/c4/IconHelpLoading_generators.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/96?cb=20170625095337" class="lazyload" /></a></span></span></span></span><span class="mobileView mobileIconLink"><a href="/wiki/Generator" title="Generator"><img alt="IconHelpLoading generators" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="32" height="32" data-image-name="IconHelpLoading generators.png" data-image-key="IconHelpLoading_generators.png" data-relevant="0" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/deadbydaylight_gamepedia_en/images/c/c4/IconHelpLoading_generators.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/32?cb=20170625095337" class="lazyload" /></a></span></span> with the most Progression explodes and <b>instantly regresses</b> by <b><span class="luaClr clr clr2" style="color: #e8c252;">10</span></b>/<b><span class="luaClr clr clr3" style="color: #199b1e;">15</span></b>/<b><span class="luaClr clr clr4" style="color: #ac3ee3;">20</span></b> <b>&#37;</b> of its total Progression.</li>
<li>Normal Generator Regression applies afterwards.</li>
<li>All Survivors repairing that Generator will scream, but not reveal their location.</li></ul>

<i>Scourge Hook: Pain Resonance</i> is disabled for the remainder of the Trial once all Tokens are consumed.
<p><i><span class="luaClr clr clr9" style="color: #e7cda2;">"The pain spills beyond flesh/darkness staining the horizon." — Girl in the Shadow by Carmina Mora</span></i></p></div>
</div>
</div>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="History">History</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fdeadbydaylight.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FScourge_Hook%3A_Pain_Resonance%3Faction%3Dedit%26section%3D1&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="tabber wds-tabber"><div class="wds-tabs__wrapper with-bottom-border"><ul class="wds-tabs"><li class="wds-tabs__tab wds-is-current" data-hash="5.4.0"><div class="wds-tabs__tab-label"><a href="#">5.4.0</a></div></li><li class="wds-tabs__tab" data-hash="6.1.0"><div class="wds-tabs__tab-label"><a href="#">6.1.0</a></div></li><li class="wds-tabs__tab" data-hash="6.1.2"><div class="wds-tabs__tab-label"><a href="#">6.1.2</a></div></li><li class="wds-tabs__tab" data-hash="6.7.0"><div class="wds-tabs__tab-label"><a href="#">6.7.0</a></div></li><li class="wds-tabs__tab" data-hash="8.0.0"><div class="wds-tabs__tab-label"><a href="#">8.0.0</a></div></li></ul></div><div class="wds-tab__content wds-is-current"><p class="mw-empty-elt">

<th width="100px"><span class="luaClr clr clr2" style="color: #e8c252;">Tier I</span></th>
<th width="100px"><span class="luaClr clr clr3" style="color: #199b1e;">Tier II</span></th>
<th width="100px"><span class="luaClr clr clr4" style="color: #ac3ee3;">Tier III</span></th>
<th>Description
</th></tr>
<tr>
<th><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/deadbydaylight_gamepedia_en/images/7/79/IconPerks_scourgeHookPainResonance.png/revision/latest?cb=20211109180802" class="image"><img alt="IconPerks scourgeHookPainResonance" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/deadbydaylight_gamepedia_en/images/7/79/IconPerks_scourgeHookPainResonance.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/64?cb=20211109180802" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="64" height="64" data-image-name="IconPerks scourgeHookPainResonance.png" data-image-key="IconPerks_scourgeHookPainResonance.png" data-relevant="1" /></a>
</th>
<td>9&#160;%
</td>
<td>12&#160;%
</td>
<td>15&#160;%
</td>
<td>Overwhelming pain reverberates outwards.
<p>At the start of the Trial, <b><span class="luaClr clr clr2" style="color: #e8c252;">4 random Hooks</span></b> are changed into <b>Scourge Hooks</b>:
</p>
<ul><li>The Auras of <b>Scourge Hooks</b> are revealed to you in <b><span class="luaClr clr clr16" style="color: #ffffff;">white</span></b>.</li></ul>
<p>Each time a Survivor is hooked on a <b>Scourge Hook</b>, the following effects apply:
</p>
<ul><li>The Generator with the most Progression explodes, instantly losing <b><span class="luaClr clr clr2" style="color: #e8c252;">9</span>/<span class="luaClr clr clr3" style="color: #199b1e;">12</span>/<span class="luaClr clr clr4" style="color: #ac3ee3;">15</span>&#160;%</b> of its Progression and starting to regress.</li>
<li>Survivors repairing that Generator will scream, revealing their location.</li></ul>
</td></tr></tbody></table><p class="mw-empty-elt"></p></div><div class="wds-tab__content"><p class="mw-empty-elt">

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Change_Log">Change Log</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fdeadbydaylight.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FScourge_Hook%3A_Pain_Resonance%3Faction%3Dedit%26section%3D2&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Patch_6.1.0"><a href="/wiki/Patch_6.1.0" class="mw-redirect" title="Patch 6.1.0">Patch 6.1.0</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fdeadbydaylight.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FScourge_Hook%3A_Pain_Resonance%3Faction%3Dedit%26section%3D3&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul><li><i><b><span class="luaClr clr clr8" style="color: #d41c1c;">Nerf</span>:</b></i> removed the <i><a href="/wiki/Loud_Noise_Notification" class="mw-redirect" title="Loud Noise Notification">Loud Noise Notification</a></i> and no longer explodes the Generator, allowing repairing Survivors to continue uninterrupted.</li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Patch_6.1.2"><a href="/wiki/Patch_6.1.2" class="mw-redirect" title="Patch 6.1.2">Patch 6.1.2</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fdeadbydaylight.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FScourge_Hook%3A_Pain_Resonance%3Faction%3Dedit%26section%3D4&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul><li><i><b><span class="luaClr clr clr2" style="color: #e8c252;">Buff</span>:</b></i> affected Generators now interrupt repairing Survivors, while still not notifying the Killer with a scream.
<ul><li>This change was motivated by a new combination of <b>Scourge Hook: Pain Resonance</b> with <a href="/wiki/Merciless_Storm" title="Merciless Storm">Merciless Storm</a><span class="iconLink" style="vertical-align: middle; padding: 0 0 0 0"><span style="width:32px;max-height: 32px" class="pcView pcIconLink"><span class="tooltip linkIncluded borderless"><span class="tooltipBaseText iconless"><a href="/wiki/Merciless_Storm" title="Merciless Storm"><img alt="IconPerks mercilessStorm" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="64" height="64" data-image-name="IconPerks mercilessStorm.png" data-image-key="IconPerks_mercilessStorm.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/deadbydaylight_gamepedia_en/images/3/36/IconPerks_mercilessStorm.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/64?cb=20220216120012" class="lazyload" /></a></span><span class="tooltiptext flex flexCenter"><span class="tooltipTextWrapper"><a href="/wiki/Merciless_Storm" title="Merciless Storm"><img alt="IconPerks mercilessStorm" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="96" height="96" data-image-name="IconPerks mercilessStorm.png" data-image-key="IconPerks_mercilessStorm.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/deadbydaylight_gamepedia_en/images/3/36/IconPerks_mercilessStorm.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/96?cb=20220216120012" class="lazyload" /></a></span></span></span></span><span class="mobileView mobileIconLink"><a href="/wiki/Merciless_Storm" title="Merciless Storm"><img alt="IconPerks mercilessStorm" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="32" height="32" data-image-name="IconPerks mercilessStorm.png" data-image-key="IconPerks_mercilessStorm.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/deadbydaylight_gamepedia_en/images/3/36/IconPerks_mercilessStorm.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/32?cb=20220216120012" class="lazyload" /></a></span></span>, which would allow a regressing Generator to trigger approximately <b>40</b> Skill Checks that the Survivor had to succeed in order to combat the Perk.</li></ul></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Patch_6.7.0"><a href="/wiki/Patch_6.7.0" class="mw-redirect" title="Patch 6.7.0">Patch 6.7.0</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fdeadbydaylight.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FScourge_Hook%3A_Pain_Resonance%3Faction%3Dedit%26section%3D5&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul><li><i><b><span class="luaClr clr clr8" style="color: #d41c1c;">Nerf</span>:</b></i> now features a Token-based system, and will only trigger if a Survivor is hooked on a <b>Scourge Hook</b> for the first time.</li>
<li><i><b><span class="luaClr clr clr2" style="color: #e8c252;">Buff</span>:</b></i> increased the Regression penalty from <b><span class="luaClr clr clr2" style="color: #e8c252;">9</span>/<span class="luaClr clr clr3" style="color: #199b1e;">12</span>/<span class="luaClr clr clr4" style="color: #ac3ee3;">15</span>&#160;%</b> to <b><span class="luaClr clr clr2" style="color: #e8c252;">15</span>/<span class="luaClr clr clr3" style="color: #199b1e;">20</span>/<span class="luaClr clr clr4" style="color: #ac3ee3;">25</span>&#160;%</b>.</li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Patch_7.5.0"><a href="/wiki/Patch_7.5.0" class="mw-redirect" title="Patch 7.5.0">Patch 7.5.0</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fdeadbydaylight.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FScourge_Hook%3A_Pain_Resonance%3Faction%3Dedit%26section%3D6&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul><li><i><b><span class="luaClr clr clr3" style="color: #199b1e;">Change</span>:</b></i> does not trigger a <i>Loud Noise Notification</i> if no Progression is lost on a <b>Generator</b>.
<ul><li>This change was due to the addition of a limit to how often individual <b>Generators</b> can experience a Regression event.</li></ul></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Patch_8.0.0"><a href="/wiki/Patch_8.0.0" class="mw-redirect" title="Patch 8.0.0">Patch 8.0.0</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fdeadbydaylight.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FScourge_Hook%3A_Pain_Resonance%3Faction%3Dedit%26section%3D7&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul><li><i><b><span class="luaClr clr clr8" style="color: #d41c1c;">Nerf</span>:</b></i> reduced the Regression penalty from <b><span class="luaClr clr clr2" style="color: #e8c252;">15</span>/<span class="luaClr clr clr3" style="color: #199b1e;">20</span>/<span class="luaClr clr clr4" style="color: #ac3ee3;">25</span>&#160;%</b> to <b><span class="luaClr clr clr2" style="color: #e8c252;">10</span>/<span class="luaClr clr clr3" style="color: #199b1e;">15</span>/<span class="luaClr clr clr4" style="color: #ac3ee3;">20</span>&#160;%</b>.</li></ul>
<p><br />
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Video">Video</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fdeadbydaylight.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FScourge_Hook%3A_Pain_Resonance%3Faction%3Dedit%26section%3D8&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>

	const useMaxDefaultContentWidth = Boolean();

	const defaultContentWidth = useMaxDefaultContentWidth ? 'expanded' : 'collapsed';

	let contentWidthPreference;

	try {
		contentWidthPreference = localStorage.getItem('contentwidth') || defaultContentWidth;
	} catch (e) {
		contentWidthPreference = defaultContentWidth;
	}

	if ( contentWidthPreference === 'expanded' ) {

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Change_Log">Change Log</span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Patch_5.3.0"><a href="/wiki/Patch_5.3.0" class="mw-redirect" title="Patch 5.3.0">Patch 5.3.0</a></span></h3>
<div class="floatleft"><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/deadbydaylight_gamepedia_en/images/d/da/IconPerks_situationalAwareness.png/revision/latest?cb=20210930143608" class="image"><img alt="IconPerks situationalAwareness" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="128" height="128" data-image-name="IconPerks situationalAwareness.png" data-image-key="IconPerks_situationalAwareness.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/deadbydaylight_gamepedia_en/images/d/da/IconPerks_situationalAwareness.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/128?cb=20210930143608" class="lazyload" /></a></div>
<ul><li><i><b><span class="luaClr clr clr13" style="color: #418284;">Retired</span></b></i>: with the departure of <a href="/wiki/CHAPTER_13:_Stranger_Things" title="CHAPTER 13: Stranger Things">CHAPTER 13: Stranger Things</a> from <i>Dead by Daylight</i>, <b>Better Together</b> was reworked into a General Survivor Perk: Situational Awareness<span class="iconLink" style="vertical-align: middle; padding: 0 0 0 0"><span style="width:32px;max-height: 32px" class="pcView pcIconLink"><span class="tooltip linkIncluded borderless"><span class="tooltipBaseText iconless"><a href="/wiki/Situational_Awareness" title="Situational Awareness"><img alt="IconPerks situationalAwareness" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="64" height="64" data-image-name="IconPerks situationalAwareness.png" data-image-key="IconPerks_situationalAwareness.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/deadbydaylight_gamepedia_en/images/d/da/IconPerks_situationalAwareness.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/64?cb=20210930143608" class="lazyload" /></a></span><span class="tooltiptext flex flexCenter"><span class="tooltipTextWrapper"><a href="/wiki/Situational_Awareness" title="Situational Awareness"><img alt="IconPerks situationalAwareness" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="96" height="96" data-image-name="IconPerks situationalAwareness.png" data-image-key="IconPerks_situationalAwareness.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/deadbydaylight_gamepedia_en/images/d/da/IconPerks_situationalAwareness.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/96?cb=20210930143608" class="lazyload" /></a></span></span></span></span><span class="mobileView mobileIconLink"><a href="/wiki/Situational_Awareness" title="Situational Awareness"><img alt="IconPerks situationalAwareness" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="32" height="32" data-image-name="IconPerks situationalAwareness.png" data-image-key="IconPerks_situationalAwareness.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/deadbydaylight_gamepedia_en/images/d/da/IconPerks_situationalAwareness.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/32?cb=20210930143608" class="lazyload" /></a></span></span>.
<ul><li>Rewrote the Lore text in the beginning of the description to be more generic.</li>
<li>This change also replaced the original icon, which showed <b>Nancy</b>, with a new one that showed a generic woman.
<ul><li>For Players who had owned <b>CHAPTER 13: Stranger Things</b> before its removal, <b>Situational Awareness</b> would still show the original icon with <b>Nancy</b>, the flavour text in the description, and the Character association with <b>Nancy</b>.</li></ul></li></ul></li></ul>
<div style="clear:both"></div>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Patch_7.3.3"><a href="/wiki/Patch_7.3.3" class="mw-redirect" title="Patch 7.3.3">Patch 7.3.3</a></span></h3>
<ul><li><i><b><span class="luaClr clr clr21" style="color: #37d1c0;">Reinstation</span></b></i>: reinstated <b>Better Together</b> with the return of <a href="/wiki/CHAPTER_13:_Stranger_Things" title="CHAPTER 13: Stranger Things">CHAPTER 13: Stranger Things</a>.
<ul><li>Renamed <b>Situational Awareness</b> back to <b>Better Together</b> and replaced the altered icon with its original one.</li>
<li>Adjusted the Lore text back to that of <b>Better Together</b>.</li></ul></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Patch_7.4.0"><a href="/wiki/Patch_7.4.0" class="mw-redirect" title="Patch 7.4.0">Patch 7.4.0</a></span></h3>
<ul><li><i><b><span class="luaClr clr clr3" style="color: #199b1e;">Change</span>:</b></i> <b>Better Together</b> is now once again a <b><span class="luaClr clr clr6" style="color: #ff8800;">Unique Perk</span></b>.</li></ul>

	const useMaxDefaultContentWidth = Boolean();

	const defaultContentWidth = useMaxDefaultContentWidth ? 'expanded' : 'collapsed';

	try {
		contentWidthPreference = localStorage.getItem('contentwidth') || defaultContentWidth;
	} catch (e) {
		contentWidthPreference = defaultContentWidth;

	if ( contentWidthPreference === 'expanded' ) {
		document.documentElement.classList.add('is-content-expanded');

</th></tr>
<tr>
<th><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/deadbydaylight_gamepedia_en/images/1/17/IconPerks_windowsOfOpportunity.png/revision/latest?cb=20180529195008" class="image"><img alt="IconPerks windowsOfOpportunity" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/deadbydaylight_gamepedia_en/images/1/17/IconPerks_windowsOfOpportunity.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/64?cb=20180529195008" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="64" height="64" data-image-name="IconPerks windowsOfOpportunity.png" data-image-key="IconPerks_windowsOfOpportunity.png" data-relevant="1" /></a>
</th>
<td>24 metres
</td>
<td>28 metres
</td>
<td>32 metres
</td>
<td>Unlocks potential in one's Aura-reading ability.
<p>The Auras of every <b>Breakable Wall</b>, <b>Pallet</b>, and <b>Windows</b> within <b><span class="luaClr clr clr2" style="color: #e8c252;">24 metres</span>/<span class="luaClr clr clr3" style="color: #199b1e;">28 metres</span>/<span class="luaClr clr clr4" style="color: #ac3ee3;">32 metres</span></b> of you are revealed to you.
</p>
</td></tr></tbody></table><p class="mw-empty-elt"></p></div></div>
<p><br />
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Change_Log">Change Log</span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Patch_3.0.0"><a href="/wiki/Patch_3.0.0" class="mw-redirect" title="Patch 3.0.0">Patch 3.0.0</a></span></h3>
<ul><li><i><b><span class="luaClr clr clr2" style="color: #e8c252;">Buff</span>:</b></i> halved the Cool-down durations from <b><span class="luaClr clr clr2" style="color: #e8c252;">60</span>/<span class="luaClr clr clr3" style="color: #199b1e;">50</span>/<span class="luaClr clr clr4" style="color: #ac3ee3;">40</span> seconds</b> to <b><span class="luaClr clr clr2" style="color: #e8c252;">30</span>/<span class="luaClr clr clr3" style="color: #199b1e;">25</span>/<span class="luaClr clr clr4" style="color: #ac3ee3;">20</span> seconds</b>.</li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Patch_5.3.0"><a href="/wiki/Patch_5.3.0" class="mw-redirect" title="Patch 5.3.0">Patch 5.3.0</a></span></h3>
<ul><li><i><b><span class="luaClr clr clr2" style="color: #e8c252;">Buff</span>:</b></i> removed the Cool-down altogether.</li>
<li><i><b><span class="luaClr clr clr2" style="color: #e8c252;">Buff</span>:</b></i> changed and increased the Aura-reading effect from a fixed <b><span class="luaClr clr clr2" style="color: #e8c252;">20 metres</span></b> across all Tiers to a variable <b><span class="luaClr clr clr2" style="color: #e8c252;">24</span>/<span class="luaClr clr clr3" style="color: #199b1e;">28</span>/<span class="luaClr clr clr4" style="color: #ac3ee3;">32</span> metres</b>.</li></ul>
<p><br />
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="_Trivia">&#160;Trivia</span></h2>
<ul><li><b>Windows of Opportunity</b> still shows an Aura for <i><b>Illusionary Pallets</b></i> and <i><b>Dream Pallets</b></i>.</li>
<li><b>Windows of Opportunity</b> still shows an Aura for Pallets and Windows blocked by The <a href="/wiki/Entity" title="Entity">Entity</a><span class="iconLink" style="vertical-align: middle; padding: 0 0 0 0"><span style="width:32px;max-height: 32px" class="pcView pcIconLink"><span class="tooltip linkIncluded borderless"><span class="tooltipBaseText iconless"><a href="/wiki/Entity" title="Entity"><img alt="IconHelp entity" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="64" height="64" data-image-name="IconHelp entity.png" data-image-key="IconHelp_entity.png" data-relevant="0" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/deadbydaylight_gamepedia_en/images/a/a9/IconHelp_entity.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/64?cb=20170907141947" class="lazyload" /></a></span><span class="tooltiptext flex flexCenter"><span class="tooltipTextWrapper"><a href="/wiki/Entity" title="Entity"><img alt="IconHelp entity" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="96" height="96" data-image-name="IconHelp entity.png" data-image-key="IconHelp_entity.png" data-relevant="0" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/deadbydaylight_gamepedia_en/images/a/a9/IconHelp_entity.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/96?cb=20170907141947" class="lazyload" /></a></span></span></span></span><span class="mobileView mobileIconLink"><a href="/wiki/Entity" title="Entity"><img alt="IconHelp entity" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="32" height="32" data-image-name="IconHelp entity.png" data-image-key="IconHelp_entity.png" data-relevant="0" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/deadbydaylight_gamepedia_en/images/a/a9/IconHelp_entity.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/32?cb=20170907141947" class="lazyload" /></a></span></span>.</li>
<li>While <a href="/wiki/Patch_7.2.0" class="mw-redirect" title="Patch 7.2.0">Patch 7.2.0</a> modified the in-game description to feature the Cool-down again that was removed in <a href="/wiki/Patch_5.3.0" class="mw-redirect" title="Patch 5.3.0">Patch 5.3.0</a>, this was merely a visual change and did not affect the Perk's effect.
<ul><li>The Developers confirmed this to be a bug.</li></ul></li></ul>
<p><br />
</p>
